# <a name="obsolete-types-in-the-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="1ca1f-102">Zastaralé typy v rozhraní .NET Framework</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1ca1f-102">Obsolete Types in the .NET Framework</span></span>
<a name="introduction"></a> <span data-ttu-id="1ca1f-103">V tabulkách v tomto článku jsou uvedeny typy, které jsou zastaralé v [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] a [!INCLUDE[net_v46](../../../includes/net-v46-md.md)]uspořádaných podle sestavení.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1ca1f-103">The tables in this article list the types that are obsolete in the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] and the [!INCLUDE[net_v46](../../../includes/net-v46-md.md)], organized by assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1ca1f-104">Pokud chcete zobrazit seznam zastaralých typů a doporučené alternativy v každé sestavení pomocí následujících odkazů.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1ca1f-104">Use the following links to see a list of the obsolete types and the recommended alternatives in each assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1ca1f-105">Protože tyto typy jsou zastaralé, jsou zastaralé také jejich členy.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1ca1f-105">Because these types are obsolete, all their members are also obsolete.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1ca1f-106">Seznam dalších zastaralé členy v knihovně tříd rozhraní .NET Framework najdete v tématu [zastaralé členy](../../../docs/framework/whats-new/obsolete-members.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1ca1f-106">For a list of additional obsolete members in the .NET Framework class library, see [Obsolete Members](../../../docs/framework/whats-new/obsolete-members.md).</span></span>

<a name="obsolete_types_in_system_assemblies"></a>
## <a name="obsolete-types-in-system-assemblies"></a><span data-ttu-id="1ca1f-133">Zastaralé typy v systému sestavení</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1ca1f-133">Obsolete Types in System Assemblies</span></span>
 <span data-ttu-id="1ca1f-134">V následujících tabulkách jsou uvedeny typy, které byly prohlášeny za zastaralé v systému sestavení.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1ca1f-134">The following tables list the types that have been declared obsolete in system assemblies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1ca1f-135">Tato sestavení se používají pro obecné\-účely vývoje aplikací, které cílí na .NET Framework.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1ca1f-135">These assemblies are used for general\-purpose application development that targets the .NET Framework.</span></span>
